% !TeX TS-program = lualatex
% !TeX spellcheck = it_IT
% !TeX encoding = UTF-8
\documentclass[11pt,a4paper]{article}
\usepackage{fontspec}
\usepackage{polyglossia} % Gestione multilingue avanzata
\usepackage{lipsum}
\usepackage{xcolor}
\usepackage{tcolorbox}
\usepackage{geometry}
\usepackage{fancyhdr}
\usepackage{hyperref}
\usepackage{booktabs}
\usepackage{multicol}

\setmainlanguage{italian}
% Definisci le lingue secondarie necessarie per il test dei font complessi
\setotherlanguage{latin}
\setotherlanguage{arabic}
\setotherlanguage{hebrew}
\setotherlanguage{japanese}
\setotherlanguage{chinese}  % Aggiunto Cinese
\setotherlanguage{hindi}    % Aggiunto Hindi
\setotherlanguage{thai}

\geometry{margin=2cm}

% Colori
\definecolor{titlecolor}{HTML}{667eea}
\definecolor{boxcolor}{HTML}{f0f0f0}
\definecolor{successcolor}{HTML}{28a745}
\definecolor{errorcolor}{HTML}{dc3545}
\definecolor{othercolor}{HTML}{0d6efd}

% Setup Box
\tcbuselibrary{skins}
\newtcolorbox{fontbox}[1]{
    colback=boxcolor, colframe=titlecolor, boxrule=1pt, arc=3pt,
    title={\textbf{#1}}, coltitle=white, colbacktitle=titlecolor
}
\newtcolorbox{errorbox}[1]{
    colback=errorcolor!10, colframe=errorcolor!80!black, boxrule=1pt, arc=3pt,
    title={\textbf{Non Caricato: #1}}, coltitle=white, colbacktitle=errorcolor!80!black
}

% --- MACRO PER CARATTERI NON LATINI (FIXED) ---
% #1: Font Name, #2: Language Tag (polyglossia), #3: Font Options (e.g., Script=Arabic), #4: Sample Text
\newcommand{\TestNonLatin}[4]{%
	\par\noindent\textbf{Test in Lingua (\texttt{#2}) con Opzioni: \texttt{[#3]}}

	\foreignlanguage{#2}{%
		\fontspec{#1}[#3]%
		#4\par
	}%
	\vspace{0.5em}
}
% --------------------------------------

% --- GESTIONE CONTATORI E INDICI ---
\newcounter{cntWorking}
\newcounter{cntBroken}
\newcounter{cntExcluded}
\setcounter{cntWorking}{0}
\setcounter{cntBroken}{0}
\setcounter{cntExcluded}{0}

% Definiamo file di output temporanei per gli indici
\newwrite\fileWorking
\immediate\openout\fileWorking=\jobname.working
\newwrite\fileBroken
\immediate\openout\fileBroken=\jobname.broken
\newwrite\fileExcluded
\immediate\openout\fileExcluded=\jobname.excluded

% Macro ROBUSTE per registrare i font (evita errori di espansione)
\protected\def\LogWorking#1{%
    \stepcounter{cntWorking}%
    \immediate\write\fileWorking{\unexpanded{\item} #1}%
}

\protected\def\LogBroken#1{%
    \stepcounter{cntBroken}%
    \immediate\write\fileBroken{\unexpanded{\item} #1}%
}

\protected\def\LogExcluded#1{%
    \stepcounter{cntExcluded}%
    \immediate\write\fileExcluded{\unexpanded{\item} #1}%
}
% -----------------------------------

\SetLipsumText{cicero}
\newcommand{\Li}{\lipsum[1][1-4]}

\title{\Huge\textbf{\color{titlecolor}Catalogo Font di Sistema}}
\author{Generato da Python in \texttt{Linux}}
\date{\today}

\begin{document}

\maketitle

\begin{abstract}
Questo documento cataloga i font installati.
I font problematici noti sono stati esclusi preventivamente. La compilazione Ã¨ eseguita con \textbf{LuaLaTeX}.
\end{abstract}

\tableofcontents
\newpage

\section{Catalogo Dettagliato}
\subsection{AR PL KaitiM Big5}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily SCRIPTS: HAN | LANG: N/A | TYPE: TEXT}


\IfFontExistsTF{AR PL KaitiM Big5}{%
    \LogWorking{AR PL KaitiM Big5}
    \begin{fontbox}{AR PL KaitiM Big5}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{AR PL KaitiM Big5}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{AR PL KaitiM Big5}
    \begin{errorbox}{AR PL KaitiM Big5}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

\vspace{1em}

\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Bengali Condensed ExtraBold}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Bengali Condensed ExtraBold}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Bengali Condensed ExtraBold}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Bengali Condensed ExtraBold}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Bengali Condensed ExtraBold}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Bengali Condensed ExtraBold}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Cherokee}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Cherokee}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Cherokee}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Cherokee}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Cherokee}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily SCRIPTS: UNKNOWN | LANG: N/A | TYPE: TEXT}


\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Gujarati ExtraBold}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Gujarati ExtraBold}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Gujarati ExtraBold}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Gujarati ExtraBold}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Gujarati ExtraBold}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Gujarati ExtraBold}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Hebrew Light}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Hebrew Light}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Hebrew Light}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Hebrew Light}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Hebrew Light}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Hebrew Light}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Mono SemiBold}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Mono SemiBold}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Mono SemiBold}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Mono SemiBold}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Mono SemiBold}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Mono SemiBold}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Syriac Eastern}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Syriac Eastern}

        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}

    \Li

{\footnotesize\ttfamily SCRIPTS: LATIN | LANG: N/A | TYPE: TEXT}


\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Tamil ExtraCondensed SemiBold}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Tamil ExtraCondensed SemiBold}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Tamil ExtraCondensed SemiBold}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Tamil ExtraCondensed SemiBold}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Tamil ExtraCondensed SemiBold}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Tamil ExtraCondensed SemiBold}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily SCRIPTS: LATIN | LANG: N/A | TYPE: TEXT}


\IfFontExistsTF{Noto Sans Thai Looped ExtraBold}{%
    \LogWorking{Noto Sans Thai Looped ExtraBold}
    \begin{fontbox}{Noto Sans Thai Looped ExtraBold}
        \centering \Large A B C D E 1 2 3
    \end{fontbox}
    \vspace{0.5em}
    \textbf{Test Latino (Lipsum):}
    {\mdseries\upshape\fontspec{Noto Sans Thai Looped ExtraBold}
    \Li
    }
}{
    \LogBroken{Noto Sans Thai Looped ExtraBold}
    \begin{errorbox}{Noto Sans Thai Looped ExtraBold}
        Il font risulta nel sistema ma LuaLaTeX non riesce a caricarlo.
    \end{errorbox}
}

% Chiusura file degli indici
\immediate\closeout\fileWorking
\immediate\closeout\fileBroken
\immediate\closeout\fileExcluded

\section{Riepilogo e Statistiche}

\begin{tcolorbox}[colback=white, colframe=gray]
\begin{center}
